        <div class="details">
         <h3 class="article-headline" itemprop="name headline">
          <a draggable="false" href="https://www.gadgethacks.com/how-to/generate-live-captions-for-any-streaming-video-audio-file-using-chromes-desktop-app-0384454/">
           <span class="series">
            How To
           </span>
           <span class="hide">
            :
           </span>
           Generate Live Captions for Any Streaming Video or Audio File Using Chrome's Desktop App
          </a>
         </h3>
         <aside class="meta-stats">
          <ul>
           <li class="stat stat-author">
            By
            <a draggable="false" href="https://creator.wonderhowto.com/jacpete/" itemprop="author" rel="author">
             Jake Peterson
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-timestamp">
            <i class="fa fa-clock-o">
            </i>
            <time class="localtimestamp" data-featured="2021-03-18T18:21:28" data-published="2021-03-18T18:21:00" data-revised="2021-03-18T18:21:28" datetime="2021-03-18T18:21:00" pubdate="pubdate" title="">
            </time>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://www.gadgethacks.com/">
             Gadget Hacks
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://www.gadgethacks.com/collection/music-audio-streaming/">
             Music &amp; Audio
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://www.gadgethacks.com/collection/movies-tv/">
             Movies &amp; TV
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://www.gadgethacks.com/collection/tweaks-hacks/">
             Tweaks &amp; Hacks
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://smartphones.gadgethacks.com/collection/google-chrome-tips-tricks/">
             Google Chrome 101
            </a>
           </li>
          </ul>
         </aside>
         <p itemprop="articleBody">
          Captions are great for catching every word and important sound in a movie or TV show, but now there's a way in Google Chrome's desktop browser to enjoy captions for any audio file or source. You could ensure you never mishear a comment during an online meeting, and you could even follow along to a song's lyrics on platforms that don't already have in-sync lyrics, such as SoundCloud.
         </p>
        </div>
       </article>

        <div class="details">
         <h3 class="article-headline" itemprop="name headline">
          <a draggable="false" href="https://ios.gadgethacks.com/how-to/dial-these-secret-codes-see-if-someone-is-hijacking-calls-texts-your-iphone-0384432/">

            How To
           </span>
           <span class="hide">
            :
           </span>
           Dial These Secret Codes to See if Someone Is Hijacking Calls &amp; Texts on Your iPhone
          </a>
         </h3>
         <aside class="meta-stats">
          <ul>
           <li class="stat stat-author">
            By
            <a draggable="false" href="https://creator.wonderhowto.com/tenebrism/" itemprop="author" rel="author">
             Justin Meyers
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-timestamp">
            <i class="fa fa-clock-o">
            </i>

            </time>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-views on-fire">
            <i class="fa fa-line-chart">
            </i>
            Popular
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://ios.gadgethacks.com/">
             iOS &amp; iPhone
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://www.gadgethacks.com/collection/privacy-security/">

            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">

             iOS 13
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://www.gadgethacks.com/collection/calling-texting-chatting/">
             Calling &amp; Texting
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://ios.gadgethacks.com/collection/ios-security-tips-tricks/">
             iOS Security 101
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://ios.gadgethacks.com/collection/ios-11-tips/">
             iOS 11
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://ios.gadgethacks.com/collection/ios-12-tips-news/">
             iOS 12
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://ios.gadgethacks.com/collection/ios-14-tips-news/">
             iOS 14
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://smartphones.gadgethacks.com/collection/tips-roundup-feature-lists/">
             Handy Roundups
            </a>
           </li>
          </ul>
         </aside>
         <p itemprop="articleBody">
          Malevolent hackers can divert your incoming calls and texts to any number they want, and they don't need to be a criminal mastermind to do it. Even friends and family members can reroute your incoming calls and messages so that they know exactly who's trying to reach you, and all it takes is seconds of access to your iPhone or wireless account. These secret codes can help uncover them.
         </p>

         <p itemprop="articleBody">
          The battery on your iPhone can go from 10% to completely dead in a matter of minutes, or at least it can feel that way. Apple does prepare you with an alert when you hit the 20% and 10% mark, but it's easy to forget to charge your iPhone before it dies even with those notifications. That's why you should also be notified when your battery's down to 5% remaining.
         </p>

            <time class="localtimestamp" data-featured="2021-03-16T20:42:02" data-published="2021-03-16T20:00:00" data-revised="2021-03-16T20:42:02" datetime="2021-03-16T20:00:00" pubdate="pubdate" title="">
            </time>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://android.gadgethacks.com/">
             Android
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://www.gadgethacks.com/collection/tweaks-hacks/">
             Tweaks &amp; Hacks
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://www.gadgethacks.com/collection/productivity-shortcuts/">
             Productivity &amp; Shortcuts
            </a>
           </li>
          </ul>
         </aside>
         <p itemprop="articleBody">
          Progressive Web Apps hope to one day bridge the gap between websites and apps by giving the former more access to your phone's features, but they're not very common yet. In the meantime, you can take matters into your own hands with an app that uses your system WebView to render websites in a full-screen, borderless window with a few extra features â a lot like a native Android app.
         </p>
        </div>
       </article>

       <article class="article-item has-image img-crop-zoom-rotate article-384442 theme-wh" data-article-id="384442" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
        <a class="img-crop no-video" draggable="false" href="https://null-byte.wonderhowto.com/how-to/python-bundle-can-teach-you-everything-you-need-know-0384442/" rel="nofollow">
         <img alt="" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://img.wonderhowto.com/img/06/49/63751170025501/0/python-bundle-can-teach-you-everything-you-need-know.1280x600.jpg" draggable="false" height="306" itemprop="image" src="https://img.wonderhowto.com/images/trans.gif" width="654"/>
        </a>
        <div class="details">
         <h3 class="article-headline" itemprop="name headline">
          <a draggable="false" href="https://null-byte.wonderhowto.com/how-to/python-bundle-can-teach-you-everything-you-need-know-0384442/">
           <span class="series">
            How To
           </span>
           <span class="hide">
            :
           </span>
           This Python Bundle Can Teach You Everything You Need to Know
          </a>
         </h3>
         <aside class="meta-stats">
          <ul>
           <li class="stat stat-author">
            By
            <a draggable="false" href="https://creator.wonderhowto.com/thehookup/" itemprop="author" rel="author">
             The Hookup
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-timestamp">
            <i class="fa fa-clock-o">
            </i>
            <time class="localtimestamp" data-featured="2021-03-13T02:23:06" data-published="2021-03-13T02:23:06" data-revised="2021-03-13T02:23:06" datetime="2021-03-13T02:23:06" pubdate="pubdate" title="">
            </time>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://null-byte.wonderhowto.com/">
             Null Byte
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="stat stat-site">
            <a draggable="false" href="https://null-byte.wonderhowto.com/collection/hacker-deals/">
             Hacker Deals
            </a>
           </li>
          </ul>
         </aside>
         <p itemprop="articleBody">
          Python is one of the most commonly used programming languages in the world. From data science to game design, Python appears in almost every industry that requires coding of some kind. If you're looking to get into or get promoted to a higher level in one of those industries, then your next step is to learn this versatile programming language.
         </p>
        </div>
       </article>
       <article class="article-item has-image img-crop-zoom-rotate article-294951 theme-wh" data-article-id="294951" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
        <a class="img-crop has-video" draggable="false" href="https://null-byte.wonderhowto.com/how-to/use-directional-antenna-with-esp8266-based-microcontroller-0294951/" rel="nofollow">
         <img alt="" class="lazy-img" data-src="https://img.wonderhowto.com/img/27/71/63723288292254/0/use-directional-antenna-with-esp8266-based-microcontroller.1280x600.jpg" draggable="false" height="306" itemprop="image" src="https://img.wonderhowto.com/images/trans.gif" width="654"/>
        </a>
        <div class="details">
         <h3 class="article-headline" itemprop="name headline">

            <a draggable="false" href="https://android.gadgethacks.com/collection/sideloaded-apps-apks/">
             Sideloaded Apps
            </a>
           </li>
          </ul>
         </aside>
         <p itemprop="articleBody">
          Most of you probably hate ads on your smartphone, but they're a part of modern digital life. As long as apps like Instagram are free to use, then we'll need to pay by dealing with posts, videos, and pop-ups trying to sell us stuff. Well, not necessarily, so long as you're OK with a few compromises.
         </p>
        </div>
       </article>
